if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '2d32da1a58f1afabdf6bed4314c72777de2e3ba3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '2d32da1a58f1afabdf6bed4314c72777de2e3ba3') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '2caa26c002885cfa387801254a8d0e605d8d1bb2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '2d32da1a58f1afabdf6bed4314c72777de2e3ba3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') != '5341bbba7ed10ead806fade02fca4de1c665dccb') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '5341bbba7ed10ead806fade02fca4de1c665dccb') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '6166ce1b26ae01af88235cca071d7300bb87fa7d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '5341bbba7ed10ead806fade02fca4de1c665dccb') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_8();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != 'e2ce13d3ac67908bdd77f38397fa9b7d4f590d15') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'e2ce13d3ac67908bdd77f38397fa9b7d4f590d15') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '368013a30f2e98028f26b3840301764a992c70aa') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'e2ce13d3ac67908bdd77f38397fa9b7d4f590d15') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
